2024-11-08T15:57:57Z #11 287.5 OMPI_MCA_coll_ucc_enable=1
2024-11-08T15:57:57Z #11 287.5 before launching your MPI processes.

2024-11-08T15:57:57Z #11 287.5 
2024-11-08T15:57:57Z #11 287.5 On Linux, Open MPI is built with CUDA awareness but it is disabled by default.
2024-11-08T15:57:57Z #11 287.5 To enable it, please set the environment variable
2024-11-08T15:57:57Z #11 287.5 OMPI_MCA_opal_cuda_support=true
2024-11-08T15:57:57Z #11 287.5 before launching your MPI processes.
2024-11-08T15:57:57Z #11 287.5 Equivalently, you can set the MCA parameter in the command line:
